​IJAMBO RY’IBANZE
Muririmbire Uwiteka muhimbaze izina rye,mwerekane agakiza ke uko
bukeye.
Nimuze tumuramye twunamye, Dupfukamire Uwiteka umuremyi wacu.
(Zab.96:2; 95:6)
Bene Data bakundwa Yesu ashimwe. Nanyuma y’izo ntashyo
ntitwabura gushima Imana yongeye kuduha kino gitabo gishya
cy’indirimbo cyitwa( TURIRIMIBIRE IMANA) iki gitabo gikoreshwa
mugihe cy’Iteraniro ryera: Murusengero ndetse no mungo zacu;
cyangwa mugihe cyo gusura urugo kurundi dukora ivugabutmwa (Door
to Door Evangelism), mumashuri yo kucyumweru( Sunday
school)Kwigisha abazabatizwa n’abakomezwa, no mu nama
zitandukanye. Kinakoreshwa kandi no mu mashuri ya Bibiliya
ahategurirwa abashaka kuba abavugabutumwa.
Nkuko Umwanditsi wa Zaburi avuga, iki kituyobora neza mu buryo bwo
kuririmbira Imana no kuyiramya turi mu mujyo umwe tudahuzagurika,
tugikunde kandi ibikubiyemo tuzabyubahirize kuko ar’isoko y’umugisha
kuri twe.
Ikindi nuko iki gitabo kigabanyijemo ibice bibiri by’ingenzi, igice cya
mbere kigizwe n’indirimbo igice cya kabiri ni Liturgiya na
Gatigisimu.Ntoya ya Martin Luther. Ibikubiye mur’ibyo bice byombi
birimo inyigisho zikomeye zitwibutsa inshingano zacu nk’abakristo
n’uburyo dukwiriye kwitwara imbere y’Imana yacu.
Mbifurije kuyoborwa na Mwuka Wera mu gihe cyose turirimbira Imana
kandi imitima yacu nayo ihindurwe ituro ryera rishimwa n’Imana
8

binyuze mukuririmba , kuramya no gusingiza Imana twifashije iki
gitabo.
Nsoza ndagirango nshimire itsinda rishinzwe ubwanditsi riyobowe na
Rev Dean Sarambuye Celestin Imana ibahe umugisha.
Uwanyu muri Kristo.
Bishop MUGABO Evarister
Umuyobozi Mukuru wa LCR
​IRIBURIRO
Iki gitabo cyitwa TURIRIMBIRE IMANA ni ( version)icya kabiri icya mbere
cyasohotse mu 2002 aricyo twari tugikoresha kugeza ubu. Icyakora
version ya mbere yari ntoya kandi yagaragayemo amakosa menshi
kubera ko igitabo cyakozwe twihuta kuko itorero ryari rimaze
kwemerwa rihabwa ubuzimagatozi biba ngombwa ko dushaka igitabo
cyadufasha kuyobora amateraniro nkuko twari tumenyereye kandi
nkuko itorero ry’abalutheri rikora aho rikorera hose ku isi.
Nkuko mubizi intangiriro irarushya(Mwanzo mgumu)
Iki gitabo cya kabiri rero hashize igihe kinini tugitegura twagerageje
gushyiramo gahunda nyinshi z’amasengesho dukeneye gukoresha mu
itorero , dushyira hamwe na zimwe mu ndirimbo zikunze gukoreshwa
cyane ziboneka mu gitabo cy’Indirimbo zo Gushimish’Imana mu rwego
rwo kugabanya umutwaro w’ibitabo.
Harimo indirimbo 414,Iki gitabo na Bibliya bizaba bihagije kugufasha
gukurikirana amateraniro cyangwa umuhango w’Itorero wose. Hari
indirimbo zahinduwe ziva mu zindi ndimi uzasanga ku ntangiriro

Indirimbo zo Gushimisha Imana

AGK=

Ikinyarwanda

Indirimbo z’Agakiza

Ndasaba buri wese gushishikarira gukoresha iki gitabo kugirango twese
tugendere mu murongo umwe dukomeze ubusugire bw’Itorero ryacu.
Ndashimira cyane umuntu wese uzi ko yashyize umusanzu we uwo
ariwo wose kur’iki gitabo:Ndabizi ko abenshi mwatanze
imbaraga,umbwenge,umwanya,ibitekerezo ,imitungo,inama
n’amasengesho mwese ndabibashimira hari n’ababihemberwaga
n’abitangaga buri wese Imana imukubire kenshi. Sinabura gushimira na
Mzee Bizima wahinduye mu Kinyarwanda indirimbo 5 z’igihaya ariko
hari utwo nagiye nkosoramo nduhuza n’imvugo za githeologiya.
N.B.Impine Umus.ni umusengesha Umush.Umushumba
By’umwihariko ndashimira Biro Nkuru ya LCR yabishyizemo imbaraga
ubushake n’amafranga.
Imana yuzuze ububiko itorero ritere imbere. Umuvandimwe wanyu
muri Kristo Yesu,
Rev.Dean SARAMBUYE Celestin- Ushinzwe Ubwanditsi muri LCR

N’UMWANA N’UMWUKA
WERA. AMEN
Bose. Indirimbo (bahagaze)
Umush. Uwitek’ Imana ari
kumwe natwe, nimuze twese
tumuramye kandi tumuhe
icyubahiro,twumve Ijambo rye
ritwigisha rigira riti:
Ukund’ Uwiteka Imana
yawe,n’umutima wawe
wose,n’ubugingo bwawe bwose,
n’ imbaraga zawe
zose,n’ubwenge bwawe bwose.
Kandi ukunde mugenzi wawe

nkuko wikunda.
Cyangwa
Ndi Uwiteka Imana yawe,
ntukagire izindi mana mu maso
yanjye.
Ntukavugir’ubus’izina
ry’Uwiteka Imana yawe.Ujye
wibuk’Umunsi w’ Imana no
kuwubahiriza. Wubahe so na
nyoko.Ntukice. Ntugasambane.
Ntukibe. Ntugashinj’ibinyoma
mugenzi wawe. Ntukifuz’inzu
ya mugenzi wawe, ntukifuz’
umugore wa mugenzi wawe,
cyangw’umugaragu we,
cyangw’umuja we,
cyangw’inka ye,
cyangw’indogobe ye,
cyangw’ikindi kintu cyose cya
mugenzi wawe.
Umush.
Gutabarwa
kwacu
guturuka mu izina ry’Uwiteka
Abakr. Imana yaremye ijuru
n’isi.
Umush.
Bavandimwe
muri
Kristo, mucishe bugufi Imitima
yanyu, twaturire Imana ibyaha
byacu.
KWATUR ‘IBICUMURO

BOSE:
Man’ ishobora byose, data wa
twese w’ imbabazi nyinshi.
Jyewe umunyantege nke
n’umunyabyaha, Ndicuz’
imbere yawe ibicumuro byose
nakoze; mu bitekerezo, mu
magambo mu bikorwa. Kuko
ntahwema kukubabaza
nkwiriye igihano cy’iteka.
Ariko ibyaha byanjye byose
ndabyatuye kandi mbyihannye
by’ ukuri. Ndakwinginze kubw’
ubuntu bwawe bwinshi,
Ungirir’imbabazi, unkize,
umpe umwuka wawe Wera
ngir’ imyifatire mishya Amen.
Cyangwa
Mana ishobora byose, Data wa
twese wo mw’ijuru ,ndihana ko
nagucumuyeho, ngagucumura
no kuri bagenzi bagenzi banjye,
mu bitekerezo, mu magambo
no mu bikorwa. Ndakwinginze
ungirir’ imbabazi kubw’
umwana wawe Yesu Kristo,
Umbabarire ibyaha byanjye
byose unyuhagiz’ Umwuka
wawe Wera, uhembur’
umutima wanjye, nshobore

kubabarir’ abandi mu bugingo
bushya mu cyubahiro cy’ Izina
ryawe Ryera. Amen
KUBABARIRWA IBYAHA
Umuvgbt. Imana nyir’ imbabazi
n’ ubushobozi bwose,yatugiriye
ibambe, iduha Umwana wayo w’
ikinege Yesu Kristo ngo adupfire
k’ umusaraba,kubw’ izina rye
itubabarir’ ibyaha byacu byose.
Amen
Umush. Niba mwihannye
by’ukuri kandi musab’imbabazi z’
ibyaha byanyu kubwa Yesu Kristo
mubikuye ku mutima,kubw’
ububasha bw’ ijambo rye,
ndabamenyesha yuko Imana kubw’
ubuntu bwayo ibababariye ibyaha
byanyu byose mu izina rya Data wa
twese, n’ Umwana n’ Umwuka
Wera. Amen
Bwira mugenzi wawe mwegeranye
uti: Akira imbabazi z’Imana.

ABABYEYI
N’ABISHINGIZI.
(nyuma yo kubatiza abana babo)
Umush; Mana ishobora byose,
turagushimira ubuntu bwinshi
utugirira buri munsi. Kandi
turagushimira
kubw’
aba/
uyu/ba/mu/byeyi
waragiye
ukamu/ukaba
rinda
batwite
kugeza no mu gihe cyo kubyara
nyina w’umwana aba yumva ari
hagati y’ urupfu n’ ubuzima.
Ndetse n’abagabo babo bafite
ubwoba,
ariko
ukabafasha
kubyara neza aba bana/uyu
mwana bazanye imbere yawe
n’imbere
y’ Itorero ryawe
kugaragaza ibyishimo
n’
ishimwe byabo babinjiza mu
muryango w’ abera bawe.
Hamwe n’abemeye kwishingira
aba bana bakazabafasha mu
mikurire yabo mu by’umwuka no
kubatoza imico ya gikristo
bafatanije
n’ababyeyi
babo
,ubashoboze
Mana
kubanza
kwitunganya
bo
ubwabo

iyo nshingano nshya bahawe
yiyongera kuzindi zitandukanye

basanganywe.
Turakwinginze kubw’ imbabazi
zawe

wakire

Umwana wawe kandi Umwami
wacu Yesu Kristo. Amen

Mutima wamjye, himbaza

Mwa bindimo byose mwe,
muhimbaz’ izina rye.

byose.

Umush: Ashyire ibiganza kuri
buri mubyeyi avuga ati:
Imana yakuremye irakuragira
ikakurinda amanywa n’ ijoro,
nawe ujye uyihimbaza mu izina
rya Yesu Kristo iminsi yose yo
kubaho kwawe.
Imana ishobora byose kandi y’
imbabazi nyinshi,
Iguh’ umugisha, ikurinde mu
izina rya Data wa twese
n’ Umwana n’ Umwuka Wera
Amen.

wa twese n’
Umwana n’
Umwuka Wera + Amen.

yabwiye abigishwa be
ati:“Mugende muhindure

nababwiye byose,
kandi dore ndi kumwe namwe
kugeza kumperuka y’ isi

Mwabatijwe
kugira
ngo
mwihane
ibyaha
mwakire
Umwuka Wera.nuko rero uyu
munsi mwongere kumuhabwa

wacu Yesu Kristo, nimurya
umubiri we mukanywa n’
amaraso ye, mukabyakirana
ukwizera n’ imitima ituje. None
ngaho nimuvuge isezerano ryo
kubatizwa.

imirimo ye yose n’ imigenzo ye
yose ndetse n’ ibye byose.

ngukorere iteka ryose. Amen

●​ Umush: Dusabe.

Mana y’ ubuntu n’ imbabazi
Data wa twese uri mu ijuru. ni
wowe watangije ibyiza byose
muri twe,none turakwinginga
kubw’ aba bana bawe, usohoze

​XV.GAHUNDA Y’
AMASENGESHO KU MUNSI
WO KUVA K’ URUPFU
(GUCANURA)
Umus.Intumwa Paulo
aratwigisha gushimir’ Imana mu
byago kuko ari nayo iduhumuriza
mu makuba yacu yose. Reka
twumve uko abitubwira mu
rwandiko rwe rwa kabiri
yandikiye Abakorinto (2Kor 1:
3-7) Dusome. Hashimwe Imana
y’ Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo, ni
yo na se, ari nayo Data wa twese
w’ imbabazi, n’ Imana nyir’
ihumure ryose; iduhumuriza mu
makuba yacu yose, kugira ngo
natwe tubone uko duhumuriza
abari mu makuba yose,
tubahumurisha ihumure twahawe
n’ Imana; kuko nkuko Kristo

yababajwe byadusesekayeho
cyane, niko no guhumurizwa
kwatugwijijemo na Kristo. Iyo
tubabazwa tuba tubabazwa kugira
ngo muhumurizwe no gukizwa:
kandi iyo duhumurizwa, tuba
duhumurijwe no kugira ngo
muhumurizwe namwe, mubone
uko mwihanganira imibabaro
imwe n’ iyo natwe tubabazwa. Ni
cyo gituma ibyo tubiringiyeho
bishikamye, kuko tuzi yuko ubwo
mufatanyije imibabaro,
mufatanijwe no guhumurizwa.
Dusenge.
Mwami Mana itang’ amahoro
kandi ihoraho, tuzi yuko ibibaho
byose uba ubibona, nicyo gituma
duteranira
hano
mu rugo
rwa………………………..
tukugaragariza
yuko
ntakizadutandukanya
nawe.

cyangwa urupfu. Yego urupfu
rwadutwaye
umuvandimwe
(………..) maze ku bwintege nke
z’ imibiri yacu tugira umubabaro.
None turagusaba ngo ukomeze
uhumurize umuryango wasigaye
mur’ uru rugo, uhumurize natwe

abari hano tumenye neza yuko
urupfu Atari iherezo ry’ ubugingo
bw’ abizera, ahubwo ari urutindo
bambukiraho bajya mu bwami
bwawe. Turagusaba ngo weze

gutsinda ibigeragezo duhura
nabyo byose tuzashobore guca

mu

niwe

azumvira.(Itang. 49:10)

n’utwar’
ibihugu.(Kub.24:17b)

DATA WA TWESE URI MW’IJURU .
​
Bisobanura iki?
Imana ishakako tuyigirira amatsiko tukizera
neza ko ariyo data wa twese turi abana
bayo.kandi tubone uko tuyambaza tudatinya
,nkuko abana b’igikundiro biyambaza
umubyeyi wabo.
471

IZINA RYAWE RYEZWE(Ryubahwe)

Izina
ry’Imana
ntirigira
amakemwa
.turaryiyambaza ngo ryezwe no mumitwe
.izina ry’imana ryezwa muri twe ar’uko
Ijambo ryayo ribwirijwe neza abantu
bakaryumva ,bakarifata, bakaryitondera,
bakaryubahiriza nk’uko bikwiriye bitwa
abana b’Imana .ariko abavuga-butumwa
bajijinganya nibo basuzuguza Ijambo
ry’Imana.
UBWAMI BWAWE BUZE.

Bisobanura iki?
Ubwami bw’Imana buza tutabusabye ,ariko
noneho dusabe ko buza muri twe .ubwami
bw’imana buza kugirango data wa twese wo
mw’ijuru aduhe umwuka we n’imbabazi
ze,kugirango twizere ijambo rye,turyitondere
mu nzira zose kugeza ubwo tuzagera mu
mbwami bw’ijuru.
IBYUSHAKA BIBEHO MW’ISI NKUKO
BIBAHO MW’IJURU
Bisobanura iki?
472

Imana ibyo ishaka bikorwa tutabisabye
,ariko noneho dusabe ko bikorwa muri twe
kandi iby’Imana ishaka bikorerwa muri twe
,irarikira iyobowe na satani .ibyo byose
bikatubuza kubahiriza inzira y’Imana
,bikabuza ubuntu bw’Imana kuza muri
twe.Imana ishaka no kuduha imbaraga
,mw’ijambo ryayo ,kugirango dushobore
kuyizera kuzageza gupfa.

dusabe

kubona imvura n’izuba ku gihe, kubana nabo

UTUBABARIRE IBYAHA BYACU
NKUKO NATWE TUBABARIRA
ABABITUGIRIRA
Bisobanura iki?
Turasaba data wa twese uri mw’ijuru ngo ye
kuduhora ibyaha byacu, ngo atwime ibyo
dusaba. Kuko ntidukwiye kugira icyo
duhabwa kuko duhora tumucumuraho buri
munsi. Ahubwo aatugirire imbabazi gusa.
Rero nicyo gituma natwe dukwiriye kugira

imbabazi abaducumurira bose, kuko
kubabarira abandi ariho kubabarirwa bwacu
gushingiyeho.

yose.

AMASAKARAMENTU Y’ITORERO
Umwami wacu Yesu Kristo yatubwirije
amasakaramentu abiri gusa:
1. Isakaramentu ryo kubatizwa, (Umubatizo)
Mat. 28:19-20
2. Isakaramentu ryo kwakira Ifunguro Ryera
(Guhazwa) Lk.22:19-20
1. ISAKRAMENTU RYO KUBATIZWA.

Kubatizwa ni iki?
Kubatizwa ni itegeko ryo kwezwa, amazi
ajyanye n’Ijambo ry’Imana, ntabwo ari
amazi gusa abatiza.
Iryo Jambo ni rihe?
Yesu yabwiye abigishwa be ati:”N’uko
mugende muhindura abantu bo mu mahanga
kuba abigishwa banjye mubabatize mw’Izina
rya Data wa Twese n’Umwana, n’Umwuka
476

Wera. Mubigishe mwitondera ibyo
nababwiye byose kandi dore ndi kumwe
namwe iminsi yose kugeza kumperuka
y ‘isi”.(Matayo 28 :19-20).
Kubatizwa kutumarira iki ?
Kuduhanaguraho ibyaha, kudukiza urupfu
na satani, kuduh’ubugingo budashira,
twebwe abemera amasezerano n’Ijambo
ry’Imana.

Ayo masezerano n’iryo Jambo n’ibihe ?

Uwizera, akabatizwa, niwe uzakizwa, ariko
utizera azacirwaho iteka (Mariko 16 :16).

Inyigisho zigisha abayobozi b’inteko,

ubonye mweneso. Ariko natakumvira,

abashumba n’abavugabutumwa bashya

umuteze undi cyangwa babiri, ngo Ijambo

cyangwa batatu, kandi niyanga kumvira abo,
uzabimbwire Itorero : niyanga kuryumvira
naryo, azakubeho nk’umupagani cyangwa
umukoresha w’ikoro. (Mat 18 :15-17).
INYIGISHO KU BAKRISTO

Nkuko umwepisikopi akwiriye kuba
inyangamugayo, no kuba umugabo
w’umugore umwe ; ube udakunda
igisindisha, wirinda, ugira gahunda mu
kubaho kwe, ukunda gucumbikira abashyitsi,
ufite umbwenge bwo kwigisha, utari
umunywi wa vino, cyangwa umunyarukoni,
ahubwo abe umugwaneza, utarwana, utari

492

umukunzi w’impiya, utegeka neza abo

cyangwa abamenyereye vino nyinshi,

murugo rwe, ategeka neza abana be kumvira

bakifuza indamu mbi ; ahubwo bakomeze

no kubaha rwose. (Mbese utazi gutegeka abo

ubwiru bwo kwizera, bafite imitima itabacira

murugo rwe yabasha ate kurinda Itorero

urubanza. Bakwiye kubanza kugeragezwa,

ry’Imana?) kandi ntakwiriye kuba uhindutse

maze nibatabaho umugayo, babone gukora

umukristo vuba, kugira ngo atikakaza,

umurimo w’ubudiakonikazi na bo ni uko

akagwa, agacirwa ho iteka satani yaciriweho.

babe abitonda, abatabeshyera abandi,

Kandi akwiriye gushimwa neza n’abo hanze,

abadakunda ibisindisha, bakiranuka muri

kugira ngo adahinyuka akagwa mu mutego

byose. Abadiakoni bose babe abagabo

wa satani. Kandi n’abadiakoni na bo niko

b’umugore umwe, bategeka neza bana babo

bakwiriye kuba abitonda, batari intereganya

n’abo murungo zabo. Kuko abakora neza

493

uwo murimo w’ubudiakoni bibonera

umunywarukoni cyangwa uwifuza indamu

umwanya w’icyubahiro mwiza n’ubushizi

mbi ; ahubwo, abe uwukunda gucumbikira

bw’amanga bwinshi bwo kwizera Yesu

abashyitsi, ukunda ibyiza, udashayisha,

Kristo. (1Tim 3 :2-13). Ibyo nukuvuga

ukiranuka, uwera, wirinda, kandi ukomeza

abagabo batariho umugayo, bafite umugore

ijambo ryo kwizerwa nk’uko yaryigishijwe,

umwe, bafite abana bizera, kandi bataregwa

kugira ngo abone uko ahuguza abantu

ko ari inkubaganyi cyangwa ibigande. Kuko

inyigisho nzima, no gutsinda abanyamugisha

umwesikopi akwiriye kutabaho umugayo,

impaka. Kuko hariho benshi b’ibigande,

nk’uko bikwiriye igisonga cy’Imana ; kandi

n’abashukanyi, cyane cyane mu bakebwe,

ntakwiriye kuba ikinege, cyangwa ikirara

bavuga ibitagira umumaro, bakwiriye

cyangwa umunywi w’inzoga cyangwa

kuzibwa iminwa, kuko hari imiryango

494

y’abantu bubika, bakayimaraho, bigishiriza

Mwami Mana kubw’urukundo rwawe
rutagira iherezo,waduhaye kumenya ukuri
kwawe n’impano z’ubukire bwawe udufashe
tubikoreshe nk’ibisonga byawe bikwiriye
,twitangane ubushake kandi tugusenge
ubudasiba kandi udufashe tubashe gukora
imirimo iguhesha icyubahiro udushoboze
kuyobora abantu mu kuri kwawe maze
bitegure kuzaba mu bwami bwawe iteka
ryose.Tubisabye kubwa Ysu Kristo umwami
wacu. Amen
Niba inteko irimo abadafite akazi benshi

Umus.NyagasaniMana yacu twishyize mu

yacu babayeho nabi kubera kubura
akazi.Turakwinginze ubarinde kandi ubahe
imbarag a zo kwihangana mu bihe
turimo,turasabira abayobozi bacu
ubashoboze gushaka uburyo abantu bava mu
mubabaro n’agahinda ko kutagira
akazi.Maze imirimo yose ikubahisha iboneke

Yesu Kristo umwami wacu. Amen.
